   <script>
    function func_subscribe() {
                    $("#subscribetoemail").prop("disabled", true);
                    var vemailaddress = $("#input-signup-email").val();
                    $.ajax({
                        type: "POST",
                        url: '/Home/EmailSubcription?email_address=' + vemailaddress,
                        success: function (result) {
                            linkTrack('emailSubscription');
                            //$("#mp-footer-email-form").css('display', 'none');
                            $("#mp-footer-email-message").css('display', 'block');
                            $("#mp-footer-email-message").html(result);
                            $("#subscribetoemail").prop("disabled", false);
                        },
                        error: function () {
                            $("#subscribetoemail").prop("disabled", false);
                            return true;
                        }
                    });

                    return false;
                }
   </script>
